6695        /*
6696         * Describes a change in the accessible table model.
6697         */
6698        protected class AccessibleJTableModelChange
6699            implements AccessibleTableModelChange {
6700
6701            protected int type;
6702            protected int firstRow;
6703            protected int lastRow;
6704            protected int firstColumn;
6705            protected int lastColumn;
6706
6707            protected AccessibleJTableModelChange(int type, int firstRow,
6708                                                  int lastRow, int firstColumn,
6709                                                  int lastColumn) {
6710                this.type = type;
6711                this.firstRow = firstRow;
6712                this.lastRow = lastRow;
6713                this.firstColumn = firstColumn;
6714                this.lastColumn = lastColumn;
6715            }
6716
6717            public int getType() {
6718                return type;
6719            }
6720
6721            public int getFirstRow() {
6722                return firstRow;
6723            }
6724
6725            public int getLastRow() {
6726                return lastRow;
6727            }
6728
6729            public int getFirstColumn() {
6730                return firstColumn;
6731            }
6732
6733            public int getLastColumn() {
6734                return lastColumn;
6735            }
6736        }
6737
6738        /**
6739         * Track changes to the table contents
6740         */
6741        public void tableChanged(TableModelEvent e) {
6742           firePropertyChange(AccessibleContext.ACCESSIBLE_VISIBLE_DATA_PROPERTY,
6743                              null, null);
6744           if (e != null) {
6745               int firstColumn = e.getColumn();
6746               int lastColumn = e.getColumn();
6747               if (firstColumn == TableModelEvent.ALL_COLUMNS) {
6748                   firstColumn = 0;
6749                   lastColumn = getColumnCount() - 1;
6750               }
6751
6752               // Fire a property change event indicating the table model
6753               // has changed.
6754               AccessibleJTableModelChange change =
6755                   new AccessibleJTableModelChange(e.getType(),
6756                                                   e.getFirstRow(),
6757                                                   e.getLastRow(),
6758                                                   firstColumn,
6759                                                   lastColumn);
6760               firePropertyChange(AccessibleContext.ACCESSIBLE_TABLE_MODEL_CHANGED,
6761                                  null, change);
6762            }
6763        }
6764

6922         * and the cell is rendered once again.

6929
6930        /**
6931         * Track changes to table cell selections
6932         */
6933        public void valueChanged(ListSelectionEvent e) {
6934            firePropertyChange(AccessibleContext.ACCESSIBLE_SELECTION_PROPERTY,
6935                               Boolean.valueOf(false), Boolean.valueOf(true));
6936
6937            // Using lead selection index to cover both cases: node selected and node
6938            // is focused but not selected (Ctrl+up/down)
6939            int focusedRow = JTable.this.getSelectionModel().getLeadSelectionIndex();
6940            int focusedCol = JTable.this.getColumnModel().getSelectionModel().
6941                                                    getLeadSelectionIndex();
6942
6943            if (focusedRow != previousFocusedRow ||
6944                focusedCol != previousFocusedCol){
6945                Accessible oldA = getAccessibleAt(previousFocusedRow, previousFocusedCol);
6946                Accessible newA = getAccessibleAt(focusedRow, focusedCol);
6947                firePropertyChange(AccessibleContext.ACCESSIBLE_ACTIVE_DESCENDANT_PROPERTY,
6948                                    oldA, newA);
6949                previousFocusedRow = focusedRow;
6950                previousFocusedCol = focusedCol;
6951            }
6952        }

6957    // AccessibleContext support
6958
6959        /**
6960         * Get the AccessibleSelection associated with this object.  In the
6961         * implementation of the Java Accessibility API for this class,
6962         * return this object, which is responsible for implementing the
6963         * AccessibleSelection interface on behalf of itself.
6964         *
6965         * @return this object
6966         */
6967        public AccessibleSelection getAccessibleSelection() {
6968            return this;
6969        }
6970
6971        /**
6972         * Gets the role of this object.
6973         *
6974         * @return an instance of AccessibleRole describing the role of the
6975         * object
6976         * @see AccessibleRole
6977         */
6978        public AccessibleRole getAccessibleRole() {
6979            return AccessibleRole.TABLE;
6980        }
6981
6982        /**
6983         * Returns the <code>Accessible</code> child, if one exists,
6984         * contained at the local coordinate <code>Point</code>.
6985         *
6986         * @param p the point defining the top-left corner of the
6987         *    <code>Accessible</code>, given in the coordinate space
6988         *    of the object's parent
6989         * @return the <code>Accessible</code>, if it exists,
6990         *    at the specified location; else <code>null</code>
6991         */
6992        public Accessible getAccessibleAt(Point p) {
6993            int column = columnAtPoint(p);
6994            int row = rowAtPoint(p);
6995
6996            if ((column != -1) && (row != -1)) {
6997                TableColumn aColumn = getColumnModel().getColumn(column);
6998                TableCellRenderer renderer = aColumn.getCellRenderer();
6999                if (renderer == null) {
7000                    Class<?> columnClass = getColumnClass(column);
7001                    renderer = getDefaultRenderer(columnClass);
7002                }
7003                Component component = renderer.getTableCellRendererComponent(
7004                                  JTable.this, null, false, false,
7005                                  row, column);
7006                return new AccessibleJTableCell(JTable.this, row, column,
7007                      getAccessibleIndexAt(row, column));
7008            }
7009            return null;
7010        }
7011
7012        /**
7013         * Returns the number of accessible children in the object.  If all
7014         * of the children of this object implement <code>Accessible</code>,
7015         * then this method should return the number of children of this object.
7016         *
7017         * @return the number of accessible children in the object
7018         */
7019        public int getAccessibleChildrenCount() {
7020            return (JTable.this.getColumnCount() * JTable.this.getRowCount());
7021        }
7022
7023        /**
7024         * Returns the nth <code>Accessible</code> child of the object.
7025         *
7026         * @param i zero-based index of child
7027         * @return the nth Accessible child of the object
7028         */
7029        public Accessible getAccessibleChild(int i) {
7030            if (i < 0 || i >= getAccessibleChildrenCount()) {
7031                return null;
7032            } else {
7033                // children increase across, and then down, for tables
7034                // (arbitrary decision)
7035                int column = getAccessibleColumnAtIndex(i);
7036                int row = getAccessibleRowAtIndex(i);
7037
7038                TableColumn aColumn = getColumnModel().getColumn(column);
7039                TableCellRenderer renderer = aColumn.getCellRenderer();
7040                if (renderer == null) {
7041                    Class<?> columnClass = getColumnClass(column);
7042                    renderer = getDefaultRenderer(columnClass);
7043                }
7044                Component component = renderer.getTableCellRendererComponent(
7045                                  JTable.this, null, false, false,
7046                                  row, column);
7047                return new AccessibleJTableCell(JTable.this, row, column,
7048                      getAccessibleIndexAt(row, column));
7049            }
7050        }
7051
7052    // AccessibleSelection support
7053
7054        /**
7055         * Returns the number of <code>Accessible</code> children
7056         * currently selected.
7057         * If no children are selected, the return value will be 0.
7058         *
7059         * @return the number of items currently selected
7060         */
7061        public int getAccessibleSelectionCount() {
7062            int rowsSel = JTable.this.getSelectedRowCount();
7063            int colsSel = JTable.this.getSelectedColumnCount();
7064
7065            if (JTable.this.cellSelectionEnabled) { // a contiguous block
7066                return rowsSel * colsSel;
7067
7068            } else {
7069                // a column swath and a row swath, with a shared block
7070                if (JTable.this.getRowSelectionAllowed() &&
7071                    JTable.this.getColumnSelectionAllowed()) {
7072                    return rowsSel * JTable.this.getColumnCount() +
7073                           colsSel * JTable.this.getRowCount() -
7074                           rowsSel * colsSel;
7075
7076                // just one or more rows in selection
7077                } else if (JTable.this.getRowSelectionAllowed()) {
7078                    return rowsSel * JTable.this.getColumnCount();
7079
7080                // just one or more rows in selection
7081                } else if (JTable.this.getColumnSelectionAllowed()) {
7082                    return colsSel * JTable.this.getRowCount();
7083
7084                } else {
7085                    return 0;    // JTable doesn't allow selections
7086                }
7087            }
7088        }
7089
7090        /**
7091         * Returns an <code>Accessible</code> representing the
7092         * specified selected child in the object.  If there
7093         * isn't a selection, or there are fewer children selected
7094         * than the integer passed in, the return
7095         * value will be <code>null</code>.
7096         * <p>Note that the index represents the i-th selected child, which
7097         * is different from the i-th child.
7098         *
7099         * @param i the zero-based index of selected children
7100         * @return the i-th selected child
7101         * @see #getAccessibleSelectionCount
7102         */
7103        public Accessible getAccessibleSelection(int i) {
7104            if (i < 0 || i > getAccessibleSelectionCount()) {
7105                return null;
7106            }
7107
7108            int rowsSel = JTable.this.getSelectedRowCount();
7109            int colsSel = JTable.this.getSelectedColumnCount();
7110            int rowIndicies[] = getSelectedRows();
7111            int colIndicies[] = getSelectedColumns();
7112            int ttlCols = JTable.this.getColumnCount();
7113            int ttlRows = JTable.this.getRowCount();
7114            int r;
7115            int c;
7116
7117            if (JTable.this.cellSelectionEnabled) { // a contiguous block
7118                r = rowIndicies[i / colsSel];
7119                c = colIndicies[i % colsSel];
7120                return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7121            } else {
7122
7123                // a column swath and a row swath, with a shared block
7124                if (JTable.this.getRowSelectionAllowed() &&
7125                    JTable.this.getColumnSelectionAllowed()) {
7126
7127                    // Situation:
7128                    //   We have a table, like the 6x3 table below,
7129                    //   wherein three colums and one row selected
7130                    //   (selected cells marked with "*", unselected "0"):
7131                    //
7132                    //            0 * 0 * * 0
7133                    //            * * * * * *
7134                    //            0 * 0 * * 0
7135                    //
7136
7137                    // State machine below walks through the array of
7138                    // selected rows in two states: in a selected row,
7139                    // and not in one; continuing until we are in a row
7140                    // in which the ith selection exists.  Then we return
7141                    // the appropriate cell.  In the state machine, we
7142                    // always do rows above the "current" selected row first,
7143                    // then the cells in the selected row.  If we're done
7144                    // with the state machine before finding the requested
7145                    // selected child, we handle the rows below the last
7146                    // selected row at the end.
7147                    //
7148                    int curIndex = i;
7149                    final int IN_ROW = 0;
7150                    final int NOT_IN_ROW = 1;
7151                    int state = (rowIndicies[0] == 0 ? IN_ROW : NOT_IN_ROW);
7152                    int j = 0;
7153                    int prevRow = -1;
7154                    while (j < rowIndicies.length) {
7155                        switch (state) {
7156
7157                        case IN_ROW:   // on individual row full of selections
7158                            if (curIndex < ttlCols) { // it's here!
7159                                c = curIndex % ttlCols;
7160                                r = rowIndicies[j];
7161                                return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7162                            } else {                               // not here
7163                                curIndex -= ttlCols;
7164                            }
7165                            // is the next row in table selected or not?
7166                            if (j + 1 == rowIndicies.length ||
7167                                rowIndicies[j] != rowIndicies[j+1] - 1) {
7168                                state = NOT_IN_ROW;
7169                                prevRow = rowIndicies[j];
7170                            }
7171                            j++;  // we didn't return earlier, so go to next row
7172                            break;
7173
7174                        case NOT_IN_ROW:  // sparse bunch of rows of selections
7175                            if (curIndex <
7176                                (colsSel * (rowIndicies[j] -
7177                                (prevRow == -1 ? 0 : (prevRow + 1))))) {
7178
7179                                // it's here!
7180                                c = colIndicies[curIndex % colsSel];
7181                                r = (j > 0 ? rowIndicies[j-1] + 1 : 0)
7182                                    + curIndex / colsSel;
7183                                return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7184                            } else {                               // not here
7185                                curIndex -= colsSel * (rowIndicies[j] -
7186                                (prevRow == -1 ? 0 : (prevRow + 1)));
7187                            }
7188                            state = IN_ROW;
7189                            break;
7190                        }
7191                    }
7192                    // we got here, so we didn't find it yet; find it in
7193                    // the last sparse bunch of rows
7194                    if (curIndex <
7195                        (colsSel * (ttlRows -
7196                        (prevRow == -1 ? 0 : (prevRow + 1))))) { // it's here!
7197                        c = colIndicies[curIndex % colsSel];
7198                        r = rowIndicies[j-1] + curIndex / colsSel + 1;
7199                        return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7200                    } else {                               // not here
7201                        // we shouldn't get to this spot in the code!
7202//                      System.out.println("Bug in AccessibleJTable.getAccessibleSelection()");
7203                    }
7204
7205                // one or more rows selected
7206                } else if (JTable.this.getRowSelectionAllowed()) {
7207                    c = i % ttlCols;
7208                    r = rowIndicies[i / ttlCols];
7209                    return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7210
7211                // one or more columns selected
7212                } else if (JTable.this.getColumnSelectionAllowed()) {
7213                    c = colIndicies[i % colsSel];
7214                    r = i / colsSel;
7215                    return getAccessibleChild((r * ttlCols) + c);
7216                }
7217            }
7218            return null;
7219        }
7220
7221        /**
7222         * Determines if the current child of this object is selected.
7223         *
7224         * @param i the zero-based index of the child in this
7225         *    <code>Accessible</code> object
7226         * @return true if the current child of this object is selected
7227         * @see AccessibleContext#getAccessibleChild
7228         */
7229        public boolean isAccessibleChildSelected(int i) {
7230            int column = getAccessibleColumnAtIndex(i);
7231            int row = getAccessibleRowAtIndex(i);
7232            return JTable.this.isCellSelected(row, column);
7233        }
7234
7235        /**
7236         * Adds the specified <code>Accessible</code> child of the
7237         * object to the object's selection.  If the object supports
7238         * multiple selections, the specified child is added to
7239         * any existing selection, otherwise
7240         * it replaces any existing selection in the object.  If the
7241         * specified child is already selected, this method has no effect.
7242         * <p>
7243         * This method only works on <code>JTable</code>s which have
7244         * individual cell selection enabled.
7245         *
7246         * @param i the zero-based index of the child
7247         * @see AccessibleContext#getAccessibleChild
7248         */
7249        public void addAccessibleSelection(int i) {
7250            // TIGER - 4495286
7251            int column = getAccessibleColumnAtIndex(i);
7252            int row = getAccessibleRowAtIndex(i);
7253            JTable.this.changeSelection(row, column, true, false);
7254        }
7255
7256        /**
7257         * Removes the specified child of the object from the object's
7258         * selection.  If the specified item isn't currently selected, this
7259         * method has no effect.
7260         * <p>
7261         * This method only works on <code>JTables</code> which have
7262         * individual cell selection enabled.
7263         *
7264         * @param i the zero-based index of the child
7265         * @see AccessibleContext#getAccessibleChild
7266         */
7267        public void removeAccessibleSelection(int i) {
7268            if (JTable.this.cellSelectionEnabled) {
7269                int column = getAccessibleColumnAtIndex(i);
7270                int row = getAccessibleRowAtIndex(i);
7271                JTable.this.removeRowSelectionInterval(row, row);
7272                JTable.this.removeColumnSelectionInterval(column, column);
7273            }
7274        }
7275
7276        /**
7277         * Clears the selection in the object, so that no children in the
7278         * object are selected.
7279         */
7280        public void clearAccessibleSelection() {
7281            JTable.this.clearSelection();
7282        }
7283
7284        /**
7285         * Causes every child of the object to be selected, but only
7286         * if the <code>JTable</code> supports multiple selections,
7287         * and if individual cell selection is enabled.
7288         */
7289        public void selectAllAccessibleSelection() {
7290            if (JTable.this.cellSelectionEnabled) {
7291                JTable.this.selectAll();
7292            }
7293        }

7496         */
7497        private class AccessibleTableHeader implements AccessibleTable {
7498            private JTableHeader header;

7502                this.header = header;
7503                this.headerModel = header.getColumnModel();
7504            }

7552             * Returns the Accessible at a specified row and column
7553             * in the table.
7554             *

7556             * @param column zero-based column of the table
7557             * @return the Accessible at the specified row and column
7558             */
7559            public Accessible getAccessibleAt(int row, int column) {
7560
7561
7562                // TIGER - 4715503
7563                TableColumn aColumn = headerModel.getColumn(column);
7564                TableCellRenderer renderer = aColumn.getHeaderRenderer();
7565                if (renderer == null) {
7566                    renderer = header.getDefaultRenderer();
7567                }
7568                Component component = renderer.getTableCellRendererComponent(
7569                                  header.getTable(),
7570                                  aColumn.getHeaderValue(), false, false,
7571                                  -1, column);
7572
7573                return new AccessibleJTableHeaderCell(row, column,
7574                                                      JTable.this.getTableHeader(),
7575                                                      component);
7576            }

7731        /**
7732         * Returns the description of the specified row in the table.
7733         *
7734         * @param r zero-based row of the table
7735         * @return the description of the row
7736         * @since 1.3
7737         */
7738        public Accessible getAccessibleRowDescription(int r) {
7739            if (r < 0 || r >= getAccessibleRowCount()) {
7740                throw new IllegalArgumentException(Integer.toString(r));
7741            }
7742            if (rowDescription == null) {
7743                return null;
7744            } else {
7745                return rowDescription[r];
7746            }
7747        }
7748
7749        /**
7750         * Sets the description text of the specified row of the table.
7751         *
7752         * @param r zero-based row of the table
7753         * @param a the description of the row
7754         * @since 1.3
7755         */
7756        public void setAccessibleRowDescription(int r, Accessible a) {
7757            if (r < 0 || r >= getAccessibleRowCount()) {
7758                throw new IllegalArgumentException(Integer.toString(r));
7759            }
7760            if (rowDescription == null) {
7761                int numRows = getAccessibleRowCount();
7762                rowDescription = new Accessible[numRows];
7763            }
7764            rowDescription[r] = a;
7765        }
7766
7767        /**
7768         * Returns the description of the specified column in the table.
7769         *
7770         * @param c zero-based column of the table
7771         * @return the description of the column
7772         * @since 1.3
7773         */
7774        public Accessible getAccessibleColumnDescription(int c) {
7775            if (c < 0 || c >= getAccessibleColumnCount()) {
7776                throw new IllegalArgumentException(Integer.toString(c));
7777            }
7778            if (columnDescription == null) {
7779                return null;
7780            } else {
7781                return columnDescription[c];
7782            }
7783        }
7784
7785        /**
7786         * Sets the description text of the specified column of the table.
7787         *
7788         * @param c zero-based column of the table
7789         * @param a the description of the column
7790         * @since 1.3
7791         */
7792        public void setAccessibleColumnDescription(int c, Accessible a) {
7793            if (c < 0 || c >= getAccessibleColumnCount()) {
7794                throw new IllegalArgumentException(Integer.toString(c));
7795            }
7796            if (columnDescription == null) {
7797                int numColumns = getAccessibleColumnCount();
7798                columnDescription = new Accessible[numColumns];
7799            }
7800            columnDescription[c] = a;
7801        }
7802
7803        /**
7804         * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the accessible at a
7805         * given (row, column) is selected.
7806         *
7807         * @param r zero-based row of the table
7808         * @param c zero-based column of the table
7809         * @return the boolean value true if the accessible at (row, column)
7810         *     is selected; otherwise, the boolean value false
7811         * @since 1.3
7812         */
7813        public boolean isAccessibleSelected(int r, int c) {
7814            return JTable.this.isCellSelected(r, c);
7815        }
7816
7817        /**
7818         * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the specified row
7819         * is selected.
7820         *
7821         * @param r zero-based row of the table
7822         * @return the boolean value true if the specified row is selected;
7823         *     otherwise, false
7824         * @since 1.3
7825         */
7826        public boolean isAccessibleRowSelected(int r) {
7827            return JTable.this.isRowSelected(r);
7828        }
7829
7830        /**
7831         * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the specified column
7832         * is selected.
7833         *
7834         * @param c zero-based column of the table
7835         * @return the boolean value true if the specified column is selected;
7836         *     otherwise, false
7837         * @since 1.3
7838         */
7839        public boolean isAccessibleColumnSelected(int c) {
7840            return JTable.this.isColumnSelected(c);
7841        }
7842
7843        /**
7844         * Returns the selected rows in a table.
7845         *
7846         * @return an array of selected rows where each element is a
7847         *     zero-based row of the table
7848         * @since 1.3
7849         */
7850        public int [] getSelectedAccessibleRows() {
7851            return JTable.this.getSelectedRows();
7852        }
7853
7854        /**
7855         * Returns the selected columns in a table.
7856         *
7857         * @return an array of selected columns where each element is a
7858         *     zero-based column of the table
7859         * @since 1.3
7860         */
7861        public int [] getSelectedAccessibleColumns() {
7862            return JTable.this.getSelectedColumns();
7863        }
7864
7865        /**
7866         * Returns the row at a given index into the table.
7867         *
7868         * @param i zero-based index into the table
7869         * @return the row at a given index
7870         * @since 1.3
7871         */
7872        public int getAccessibleRowAtIndex(int i) {
7873            int columnCount = getAccessibleColumnCount();
7874            if (columnCount == 0) {
7875                return -1;
7876            } else {
7877                return (i / columnCount);
7878            }
7879        }
7880
7881        /**
7882         * Returns the column at a given index into the table.
7883         *
7884         * @param i zero-based index into the table
7885         * @return the column at a given index
7886         * @since 1.3
7887         */
7888        public int getAccessibleColumnAtIndex(int i) {
7889            int columnCount = getAccessibleColumnCount();
7890            if (columnCount == 0) {
7891                return -1;
7892            } else {
7893                return (i % columnCount);
7894            }
7895        }
7896
7897        /**
7898         * Returns the index at a given (row, column) in the table.
7899         *
7900         * @param r zero-based row of the table
7901         * @param c zero-based column of the table
7902         * @return the index into the table
7903         * @since 1.3
7904         */
7905        public int getAccessibleIndexAt(int r, int c) {
7906            return ((r * getAccessibleColumnCount()) + c);
7907        }
7908
7909        // end of AccessibleTable implementation --------------------
7910
7911        /**
7912         * The class provides an implementation of the Java Accessibility
7913         * API appropriate to table cells.
7914         */
7915        protected class AccessibleJTableCell extends AccessibleContext
7916            implements Accessible, AccessibleComponent {
7917
7918            private JTable parent;
7919            private int row;
7920            private int column;
7921            private int index;
7922
7923            /**
7924             *  Constructs an <code>AccessibleJTableHeaderEntry</code>.
7925             * @since 1.4
7926             */
7927            public AccessibleJTableCell(JTable t, int r, int c, int i) {
7928                parent = t;
7929                row = r;
7930                column = c;
7931                index = i;
7932                this.setAccessibleParent(parent);
7933            }
7934
7935            /**
7936             * Gets the <code>AccessibleContext</code> associated with this
7937             * component. In the implementation of the Java Accessibility
7938             * API for this class, return this object, which is its own
7939             * <code>AccessibleContext</code>.
7940             *
7941             * @return this object
7942             */
7943            public AccessibleContext getAccessibleContext() {
7944                return this;
7945            }
7946
7947            /**
7948             * Gets the AccessibleContext for the table cell renderer.
7949             *
7950             * @return the <code>AccessibleContext</code> for the table
7951             * cell renderer if one exists;
7952             * otherwise, returns <code>null</code>.
7953             * @since 1.6
7954             */
7955            protected AccessibleContext getCurrentAccessibleContext() {
7956                TableColumn aColumn = getColumnModel().getColumn(column);
7957                TableCellRenderer renderer = aColumn.getCellRenderer();
7958                if (renderer == null) {
7959                    Class<?> columnClass = getColumnClass(column);
7960                    renderer = getDefaultRenderer(columnClass);
7961                }
7962                Component component = renderer.getTableCellRendererComponent(
7963                                  JTable.this, getValueAt(row, column),
7964                                  false, false, row, column);
7965                if (component instanceof Accessible) {
7966                    return component.getAccessibleContext();
7967                } else {
7968                    return null;
7969                }
7970            }
7971
7972            /**
7973             * Gets the table cell renderer component.
7974             *
7975             * @return the table cell renderer component if one exists;
7976             * otherwise, returns <code>null</code>.
7977             * @since 1.6
7978             */
7979            protected Component getCurrentComponent() {
7980                TableColumn aColumn = getColumnModel().getColumn(column);
7981                TableCellRenderer renderer = aColumn.getCellRenderer();
7982                if (renderer == null) {
7983                    Class<?> columnClass = getColumnClass(column);
7984                    renderer = getDefaultRenderer(columnClass);
7985                }
7986                return renderer.getTableCellRendererComponent(
7987                                  JTable.this, null, false, false,
7988                                  row, column);
7989            }
7990
7991        // AccessibleContext methods
7992
7993            /**
7994             * Gets the accessible name of this object.
7995             *
7996             * @return the localized name of the object; <code>null</code>
7997             *     if this object does not have a name
7998             */
7999            public String getAccessibleName() {
8000                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8001                if (ac != null) {
8002                    String name = ac.getAccessibleName();
8003                    if ((name != null) && (name != "")) {
8004                        // return the cell renderer's AccessibleName
8005                        return name;
8006                    }
8007                }
8008                if ((accessibleName != null) && (accessibleName != "")) {
8009                    return accessibleName;
8010                } else {
8011                    // fall back to the client property
8012                    return (String)getClientProperty(AccessibleContext.ACCESSIBLE_NAME_PROPERTY);
8013                }
8014            }
8015
8016            /**
8017             * Sets the localized accessible name of this object.
8018             *
8019             * @param s the new localized name of the object
8020             */
8021            public void setAccessibleName(String s) {
8022                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8023                if (ac != null) {
8024                    ac.setAccessibleName(s);
8025                } else {
8026                    super.setAccessibleName(s);
8027                }
8028            }
8029
8030            //
8031            // *** should check toolTip text for desc. (needs MouseEvent)
8032            //
8033            /**
8034             * Gets the accessible description of this object.
8035             *
8036             * @return the localized description of the object;
8037             *     <code>null</code> if this object does not have
8038             *     a description
8039             */
8040            public String getAccessibleDescription() {
8041                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8042                if (ac != null) {
8043                    return ac.getAccessibleDescription();
8044                } else {
8045                    return super.getAccessibleDescription();
8046                }
8047            }
8048
8049            /**
8050             * Sets the accessible description of this object.
8051             *
8052             * @param s the new localized description of the object
8053             */
8054            public void setAccessibleDescription(String s) {
8055                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8056                if (ac != null) {
8057                    ac.setAccessibleDescription(s);
8058                } else {
8059                    super.setAccessibleDescription(s);
8060                }
8061            }
8062
8063            /**
8064             * Gets the role of this object.
8065             *
8066             * @return an instance of <code>AccessibleRole</code>
8067             *      describing the role of the object
8068             * @see AccessibleRole
8069             */
8070            public AccessibleRole getAccessibleRole() {
8071                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8072                if (ac != null) {
8073                    return ac.getAccessibleRole();
8074                } else {
8075                    return AccessibleRole.UNKNOWN;
8076                }
8077            }
8078
8079            /**
8080             * Gets the state set of this object.
8081             *
8082             * @return an instance of <code>AccessibleStateSet</code>
8083             *     containing the current state set of the object
8084             * @see AccessibleState
8085             */
8086            public AccessibleStateSet getAccessibleStateSet() {
8087                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8088                AccessibleStateSet as = null;
8089
8090                if (ac != null) {
8091                    as = ac.getAccessibleStateSet();
8092                }
8093                if (as == null) {
8094                    as = new AccessibleStateSet();
8095                }
8096                Rectangle rjt = JTable.this.getVisibleRect();
8097                Rectangle rcell = JTable.this.getCellRect(row, column, false);
8098                if (rjt.intersects(rcell)) {
8099                    as.add(AccessibleState.SHOWING);
8100                } else {
8101                    if (as.contains(AccessibleState.SHOWING)) {
8102                         as.remove(AccessibleState.SHOWING);
8103                    }
8104                }
8105                if (parent.isCellSelected(row, column)) {
8106                    as.add(AccessibleState.SELECTED);
8107                } else if (as.contains(AccessibleState.SELECTED)) {
8108                    as.remove(AccessibleState.SELECTED);
8109                }
8110                if ((row == getSelectedRow()) && (column == getSelectedColumn())) {
8111                    as.add(AccessibleState.ACTIVE);
8112                }
8113                as.add(AccessibleState.TRANSIENT);
8114                return as;
8115            }
8116

8118             * Gets the <code>Accessible</code> parent of this object.
8119             *
8120             * @return the Accessible parent of this object;
8121             *     <code>null</code> if this object does not
8122             *     have an <code>Accessible</code> parent
8123             */
8124            public Accessible getAccessibleParent() {
8125                return parent;
8126            }

8155             * object.
8156             *

8158             * @return the <code>Accessible</code> child of the object
8159             */

8161                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8162                if (ac != null) {
8163                    Accessible accessibleChild = ac.getAccessibleChild(i);
8164                    ac.setAccessibleParent(this);
8165                    return accessibleChild;
8166                } else {
8167                    return null;
8168                }

8493            /**
8494             * Determines if this object is visible.  Note: this means that the
8495             * object intends to be visible; however, it may not in fact be
8496             * showing on the screen because one of the objects that this object
8497             * is contained by is not visible.  To determine if an object is
8498             * showing on the screen, use <code>isShowing</code>.
8499             *
8500             * @return true if object is visible; otherwise, false
8501             */
8502            public boolean isVisible() {
8503                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8504                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
8505                    return ((AccessibleComponent) ac).isVisible();
8506                } else {
8507                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
8508                    if (c != null) {
8509                        return c.isVisible();
8510                    } else {
8511                        return false;
8512                    }
8513                }
8514            }
8515
8516            /**
8517             * Sets the visible state of the object.
8518             *
8519             * @param b if true, shows this object; otherwise, hides it
8520             */
8521            public void setVisible(boolean b) {
8522                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8523                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
8524                    ((AccessibleComponent) ac).setVisible(b);
8525                } else {
8526                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
8527                    if (c != null) {
8528                        c.setVisible(b);
8529                    }
8530                }
8531            }
8532
8533            /**
8534             * Determines if the object is showing.  This is determined
8535             * by checking the visibility of the object and ancestors
8536             * of the object.  Note: this will return true even if the
8537             * object is obscured by another (for example,
8538             * it happens to be underneath a menu that was pulled down).
8539             *
8540             * @return true if the object is showing; otherwise, false
8541             */
8542            public boolean isShowing() {
8543                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8544                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
8545                    if (ac.getAccessibleParent() != null) {
8546                        return ((AccessibleComponent) ac).isShowing();
8547                    } else {
8548                        // Fixes 4529616 - AccessibleJTableCell.isShowing()
8549                        // returns false when the cell on the screen
8550                        // if no parent
8551                        return isVisible();
8552                    }
8553                } else {
8554                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
8555                    if (c != null) {
8556                        return c.isShowing();
8557                    } else {
8558                        return false;
8559                    }
8560                }
8561            }
8562
8563            /**
8564             * Checks whether the specified point is within this
8565             * object's bounds, where the point's x and y coordinates
8566             * are defined to be relative to the coordinate system of
8567             * the object.
8568             *
8569             * @param p the <code>Point</code> relative to the
8570             *    coordinate system of the object
8571             * @return true if object contains <code>Point</code>;
8572             *    otherwise false
8573             */
8574            public boolean contains(Point p) {
8575                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8576                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
8577                    Rectangle r = ((AccessibleComponent) ac).getBounds();
8578                    return r.contains(p);
8579                } else {
8580                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
8581                    if (c != null) {
8582                        Rectangle r = c.getBounds();
8583                        return r.contains(p);
8584                    } else {
8585                        return getBounds().contains(p);
8586                    }
8587                }
8588            }
8589
8590            /**
8591             * Returns the location of the object on the screen.
8592             *
8593             * @return location of object on screen -- can be
8594             *    <code>null</code> if this object is not on the screen
8595             */
8596            public Point getLocationOnScreen() {
8597                if (parent != null && parent.isShowing()) {
8598                    Point parentLocation = parent.getLocationOnScreen();
8599                    Point componentLocation = getLocation();
8600                    componentLocation.translate(parentLocation.x, parentLocation.y);
8601                    return componentLocation;
8602                } else {
8603                    return null;
8604                }
8605            }
8606

8618                if (parent != null) {
8619                    Rectangle r = parent.getCellRect(row, column, false);
8620                    if (r != null) {
8621                        return r.getLocation();
8622                    }
8623                }
8624                return null;
8625            }
8626

8630            public void setLocation(Point p) {
8631//              if ((parent != null)  && (parent.contains(p))) {

8634            }

8752            /**

8754             *
8755             * @param row header cell row index
8756             * @param column header cell column index
8757             * @param parent header cell parent
8758             * @param rendererComponent component that renders the header cell
8759             */
8760            public AccessibleJTableHeaderCell(int row, int column,
8761                                              JTableHeader parent,
8762                                              Component rendererComponent) {
8763                this.row = row;
8764                this.column = column;
8765                this.parent = parent;
8766                this.rendererComponent = rendererComponent;
8767                this.setAccessibleParent(parent);
8768            }

8773             * API for this class, return this object, which is its own
8774             * <code>AccessibleContext</code>.

8776             * @return this object
8777             */
8778            public AccessibleContext getAccessibleContext() {
8779                return this;
8780            }

8784             * renderer.

8788            }

8800             * Gets the accessible name of this object.
8801             *
8802             * @return the localized name of the object; <code>null</code>
8803             *     if this object does not have a name
8804             */
8805            public String getAccessibleName() {
8806                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8807                if (ac != null) {
8808                    String name = ac.getAccessibleName();
8809                    if ((name != null) && (name != "")) {
8810                        return ac.getAccessibleName();
8811                    }
8812                }
8813                if ((accessibleName != null) && (accessibleName != "")) {
8814                    return accessibleName;
8815                } else {
8816                    return null;
8817                }
8818            }

8865             * Gets the role of this object.
8866             *
8867             * @return an instance of <code>AccessibleRole</code>
8868             *      describing the role of the object
8869             * @see AccessibleRole
8870             */
8871            public AccessibleRole getAccessibleRole() {
8872                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8873                if (ac != null) {
8874                    return ac.getAccessibleRole();
8875                } else {
8876                    return AccessibleRole.UNKNOWN;
8877                }
8878            }
8879
8880            /**
8881             * Gets the state set of this object.
8882             *
8883             * @return an instance of <code>AccessibleStateSet</code>
8884             *     containing the current state set of the object
8885             * @see AccessibleState
8886             */
8887            public AccessibleStateSet getAccessibleStateSet() {
8888                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
8889                AccessibleStateSet as = null;
8890
8891                if (ac != null) {
8892                    as = ac.getAccessibleStateSet();
8893                }
8894                if (as == null) {
8895                    as = new AccessibleStateSet();
8896                }
8897                Rectangle rjt = JTable.this.getVisibleRect();
8898                Rectangle rcell = JTable.this.getCellRect(row, column, false);
8899                if (rjt.intersects(rcell)) {
8900                    as.add(AccessibleState.SHOWING);
8901                } else {
8902                    if (as.contains(AccessibleState.SHOWING)) {
8903                         as.remove(AccessibleState.SHOWING);
8904                    }
8905                }
8906                if (JTable.this.isCellSelected(row, column)) {
8907                    as.add(AccessibleState.SELECTED);
8908                } else if (as.contains(AccessibleState.SELECTED)) {
8909                    as.remove(AccessibleState.SELECTED);
8910                }
8911                if ((row == getSelectedRow()) && (column == getSelectedColumn())) {
8912                    as.add(AccessibleState.ACTIVE);
8913                }
8914                as.add(AccessibleState.TRANSIENT);
8915                return as;
8916            }
8917

9246                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
9247                    return ((AccessibleComponent) ac).getFontMetrics(f);
9248                } else {
9249                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
9250                    if (c != null) {
9251                        return c.getFontMetrics(f);
9252                    } else {
9253                        return null;
9254                    }
9255                }
9256            }

9294            /**
9295             * Determines if this object is visible.  Note: this means that the
9296             * object intends to be visible; however, it may not in fact be
9297             * showing on the screen because one of the objects that this object
9298             * is contained by is not visible.  To determine if an object is
9299             * showing on the screen, use <code>isShowing</code>.
9300             *
9301             * @return true if object is visible; otherwise, false
9302             */
9303            public boolean isVisible() {
9304                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
9305                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
9306                    return ((AccessibleComponent) ac).isVisible();
9307                } else {
9308                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
9309                    if (c != null) {
9310                        return c.isVisible();
9311                    } else {
9312                        return false;
9313                    }
9314                }
9315            }

9317            /**
9318             * Sets the visible state of the object.
9319             *
9320             * @param b if true, shows this object; otherwise, hides it
9321             */
9322            public void setVisible(boolean b) {
9323                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
9324                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
9325                    ((AccessibleComponent) ac).setVisible(b);
9326                } else {
9327                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
9328                    if (c != null) {
9329                        c.setVisible(b);
9330                    }
9331                }
9332            }
9333
9334            /**
9335             * Determines if the object is showing.  This is determined
9336             * by checking the visibility of the object and ancestors
9337             * of the object.  Note: this will return true even if the
9338             * object is obscured by another (for example,
9339             * it happens to be underneath a menu that was pulled down).
9340             *
9341             * @return true if the object is showing; otherwise, false
9342             */
9343            public boolean isShowing() {
9344                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
9345                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
9346                    if (ac.getAccessibleParent() != null) {
9347                        return ((AccessibleComponent) ac).isShowing();
9348                    } else {
9349                        // Fixes 4529616 - AccessibleJTableCell.isShowing()
9350                        // returns false when the cell on the screen
9351                        // if no parent
9352                        return isVisible();
9353                    }
9354                } else {
9355                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
9356                    if (c != null) {
9357                        return c.isShowing();
9358                    } else {
9359                        return false;
9360                    }
9361                }
9362            }
9363
9364            /**
9365             * Checks whether the specified point is within this
9366             * object's bounds, where the point's x and y coordinates
9367             * are defined to be relative to the coordinate system of
9368             * the object.
9369             *
9370             * @param p the <code>Point</code> relative to the
9371             *    coordinate system of the object
9372             * @return true if object contains <code>Point</code>;
9373             *    otherwise false
9374             */
9375            public boolean contains(Point p) {
9376                AccessibleContext ac = getCurrentAccessibleContext();
9377                if (ac instanceof AccessibleComponent) {
9378                    Rectangle r = ((AccessibleComponent) ac).getBounds();
9379                    return r.contains(p);
9380                } else {
9381                    Component c = getCurrentComponent();
9382                    if (c != null) {
9383                        Rectangle r = c.getBounds();
9384                        return r.contains(p);
9385                    } else {
9386                        return getBounds().contains(p);
9387                    }
9388                }
9389            }
9390
9391            /**
9392             * Returns the location of the object on the screen.
9393             *
9394             * @return location of object on screen -- can be
9395             *    <code>null</code> if this object is not on the screen
9396             */
9397            public Point getLocationOnScreen() {
9398                if (parent != null && parent.isShowing()) {
9399                    Point parentLocation = parent.getLocationOnScreen();
9400                    Point componentLocation = getLocation();
9401                    componentLocation.translate(parentLocation.x, parentLocation.y);
9402                    return componentLocation;
9403                } else {
9404                    return null;
9405                }
9406            }
9407
9408            /**
9409             * Gets the location of the object relative to the parent
9410             * in the form of a point specifying the object's
9411             * top-left corner in the screen's coordinate space.
9412             *
9413             * @return an instance of <code>Point</code> representing
9414             *    the top-left corner of the object's bounds in the
9415             *    coordinate space of the screen; <code>null</code> if
9416             *    this object or its parent are not on the screen
9417             */
9418            public Point getLocation() {
9419                if (parent != null) {
9420                    Rectangle r = parent.getHeaderRect(column);
9421                    if (r != null) {
9422                        return r.getLocation();
9423                    }
9424                }
9425                return null;
9426            }
9427

9431             * @see #getLocation
9432             */
9433            public void setLocation(Point p) {
9434            }
